       <header class="entry-header">
        <h1 class="entry-title">
         5 moments only a fly fisherman would understand
        </h1>
        <div class="entry-meta">
         <span class="date">
          <a href="http://blog.fishtec.co.uk/5-moments-fly-fishing" rel="bookmark" title="Permalink to 5 moments only a fly fisherman would understand">
           <time class="entry-date" datetime="2013-07-11T09:09:24+00:00">
            July 11, 2013
           </time>
          </a>
         </span>
         <span class="categories-links">
          <a href="http://blog.fishtec.co.uk/category/fly-fishing" rel="category tag">
           Fly Fishing
          </a>
         </span>
         <span class="author vcard">
          <a class="url fn n" href="http://blog.fishtec.co.uk/author/jules-anthony" rel="author" title="View all posts by Jules Anthony">
           Jules Anthony

        <p>
         <strong>
          It has been said that the world can be divided into two camps: those who love fly fishing, and those who havent tried it yet.
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         Its an enjoyable, challenging sport, which lures people in from all walks of life and gets them hooked. There are magic moments to be had, that only a fly fisherman would understand.
        </p>
        <h3>
         The beautiful silence
        </h3>
        <div class="wp-caption aligncenter" id="attachment_9228" style="width: 535px">
         <img alt="Contemplative" class="size-full wp-image-9228" data-lazy-src="http://blog.fishtec.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/Fishing-sunset.jpg" height="394" src="http://blog.fishtec.co.uk/wp-content/plugins/speed-booster-pack/inc/images/1x1.trans.gif" width="525"/>
         <noscript>
          <img alt="Contemplative" class="size-full wp-image-9228" height="394" src="http://blog.fishtec.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/Fishing-sunset.jpg" width="525"/>
         </noscript>
         <p class="wp-caption-text">
          <strong>
           Feeling contemplative
          </strong>
          <br/>
          Source:
          <a href="http://www.militarymentalhealth.org/blog/wp-content/uploads/2012/03/fishing-image.jpg" onclick="_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.militarymentalhealth.org/blog/wp-content/uploads/2012/03/fishing-image.jpg', 'Military Mental Health']);">
           Military Mental Health
          </a>
         </p>
        </div>
        <p>
         Author Izaak Walton called fly fishing the contemplative mans recreation. When youre out there alone with your
         <a href="http://www.fishtec.co.uk/shop.cfm/fly-fishing/fly-rods/40/6020">
          fly fishing rod
         </a>
         , watching the evening mist creep over the river, well its only natural to feel contemplative.
        </p>
        <p>
         The beautiful silence is about the seclusion and beauty of nature fusing with the calm, focused mind of the fly fisherman. Simply peaceful is the best way to describe it.
        </p>
        <p>
         The sound of a can of beer being opened can sometimes break the beautiful silence, but only for a few seconds.
        </p>
        <h3>
         Lost in the challenge
        </h3>
        <div class="wp-caption aligncenter" id="attachment_9230" style="width: 535px">
         <img alt="Lost in the moment" class="size-full wp-image-9230" data-lazy-src="http://blog.fishtec.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/Lost-in-the-moment.jpg" height="349" src="http://blog.fishtec.co.uk/wp-content/plugins/speed-booster-pack/inc/images/1x1.trans.gif" width="525"/>
         <noscript>
          <img alt="Lost in the moment" class="size-full wp-image-9230" height="349" src="http://blog.fishtec.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/Lost-in-the-moment.jpg" width="525"/>
         </noscript>
         <p class="wp-caption-text">
          <strong>
           Lost in the moment
          </strong>
          <br/>
          Source:
          <a href="http://www.valleysprings.co.uk/sports-local-to-valley-springs" onclick="_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.valleysprings.co.uk/sports-local-to-valley-springs', 'Valley Springs']);">
           Valley Springs
          </a>
         </p>
        </div>
        <p>
         Every river and location presents a new challenge. The fly fisherman must find the correct approach and have patience in order to have success.
        </p>
        <p>
         It can be utterly engrossing when your mind is completely focused on the challenge. How strong is that wind? Wheres the fish holding? Am I using the right fly? Whats the depth of the fly?
        </p>
        <p>
         Half an hour speeds by, one hour, two hours and you are lost in the challenge  engaged and involved with the hunt.
        </p>
        <p>
         Maybe you win, maybe not, either way  every fish is a new lesson.
        </p>
        <h3>
         Spots
        </h3>
        <div class="wp-caption aligncenter" id="attachment_9231" style="width: 535px">
         <img alt="Home from home" class="size-full wp-image-9231" data-lazy-src="http://blog.fishtec.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/Fishing-home-from-home.jpg" height="394" src="http://blog.fishtec.co.uk/wp-content/plugins/speed-booster-pack/inc/images/1x1.trans.gif" width="525"/>
         <noscript>
          <img alt="Home from home" class="size-full wp-image-9231" height="394" src="http://blog.fishtec.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/Fishing-home-from-home.jpg" width="525"/>
         </noscript>
         <p class="wp-caption-text">
          <strong>
           Home from home
          </strong>
          <br/>
          Source:
          <a href="http://www.wallpaperhere.com/Lake_Hut_96761/download_800x600" onclick="_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.wallpaperhere.com/Lake_Hut_96761/download_800x600', 'Wallpaper Here']);">
           Wallpaper Here
          </a>
         </p>
        </div>
        <p>
         Every fly fisherman has a favourite spot. Whether its the landscape, the location or the fish on offer, its mightily comforting to spend a lot of time in ones own spot. A home from home if you like.
        </p>
        <p>
         But sometimes you hear of a new spot to explore. Packing up your fishing vehicle with bivvy, fishing gear and refreshments and setting off to a new location can feel most exhilarating.
        </p>
        <p>
         And it will most likely be a stunning spot too as fly-fishing takes you to some of the most beautiful places one can imagine.
        </p>
        <h3>
         Connecting to nature
        </h3>
        <div class="wp-caption aligncenter" id="attachment_9232" style="width: 535px">
         <img alt="At one with nature" class="size-full wp-image-9232" data-lazy-src="http://blog.fishtec.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/Kingfisher.jpeg" height="339" src="http://blog.fishtec.co.uk/wp-content/plugins/speed-booster-pack/inc/images/1x1.trans.gif" width="525"/>
         <noscript>
          <img alt="At one with nature" class="size-full wp-image-9232" height="339" src="http://blog.fishtec.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/Kingfisher.jpeg" width="525"/>
         </noscript>
         <p class="wp-caption-text">
          <strong>
           At one with nature
          </strong>
          <br/>
          Source:
          <a href="http://www.wakingtimes.com/2012/10/22/void-of-silence/kingfisher-fish_1007458i/" onclick="_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.wakingtimes.com/2012/10/22/void-of-silence/kingfisher-fish_1007458i/', 'Waking Times']);">
           Waking Times
          </a>
         </p>
        </div>
        <p>
         You dont have to be a tree hugger to appreciate how rewarding it is to feel connected to nature.
        </p>
        <p>
         Fly-fishing provides a wonderful excuse to experience some truly stunning, Zen-like moments and gets you close to the core of what it is to be human.
        </p>
        <p>
         Watching birds fly past the sunset whilst youre waist high in water, allowing a curious dragonfly to land on your fly-fishing rod, spotting a deer come down to the river for a drink as the morning mist circles around you  fly fishing puts you at one with nature.
        </p>
        <h3>
         The catch
        </h3>
        <div class="wp-caption aligncenter" id="attachment_9249" style="width: 535px">
         <img alt="fly fishing catch" class="size-full wp-image-9249" data-lazy-src="http://blog.fishtec.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/fly-fishing-catch.jpg" height="376" src="http://blog.fishtec.co.uk/wp-content/plugins/speed-booster-pack/inc/images/1x1.trans.gif" width="525"/>
         <noscript>
          <img alt="fly fishing catch" class="size-full wp-image-9249" height="376" src="http://blog.fishtec.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/fly-fishing-catch.jpg" width="525"/>
         </noscript>
         <p class="wp-caption-text">
          <strong>
           The smile says it all
          </strong>
          <br/>
          Source:
          <a href="http://flyfishing.thefuntimesguide.com/2008/03/fly_fishing_cprcatch_photograp.php" onclick="_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://flyfishing.thefuntimesguide.com/2008/03/fly_fishing_cprcatch_photograp.php', 'The Fun Times Guide']);">
           The Fun Times Guide
          </a>
         </p>
        </div>
        <p>
         For many  especially beginners who are keen for instant results, the success of a fly-fishing session is measured by what is caught.
        </p>
        <p>
         Even those that say they prefer the game and the process rather than the catch, still require that magic bite from the fish to confirm their ability.
        </p>
        <p>
         After youve invested a lot of time, skill and practice nothing beats the feeling when you see that fly dip and feel a tug.
        </p>
        <p>
         The sheer joy of landing a fish has to be the most magical moment of all.
        </p>
        <div class="yarpp-related">
         <h3>
          Related posts:
         </h3>
         <ol>
          <li>
           <a href="http://blog.fishtec.co.uk/fishing-the-river-monnow" rel="bookmark" title="Fishing the River Monnow">

            Find a fly fishing instructor

           </a>
          </li>

           <a href="http://blog.fishtec.co.uk/iain-barrs-april" rel="bookmark" title="Iain Barrs April Fly fishing Diary">

           </a>

        </div>
       </div>

/*  Collapse Functions, version 2.0
 *
 *--------------------------------------------------------------------------*/
String.prototype.trim = function() {
  return this.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,"");
}

function createCookie(name,value,days) {
  if (days) {
    var date = new Date();
    date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000));
    var expires = "; expires="+date.toGMTString();
  } else {
    var expires = "";
  }
  document.cookie = name+"="+value+expires+"; path=/";
}

function readCookie(name) {
  var nameEQ = name + "=";
  var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
  for(var i=0;i &lt; ca.length;i++) {
    var c = ca[i];
    while (c.charAt(0)==' ') {
      c = c.substring(1,c.length);
    }
    if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) {
      return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
    }
  }
  return null;
}

function eraseCookie(name) {
  createCookie(name,"",-1);
}

function addExpandCollapse(id, expandSym, collapseSym, accordion) {
  jQuery('#' + id + ' .expand').live('click', function() {
    if (accordion==1) {
      var theDiv = jQuery(this).parent().parent().find('span.collapse').parent().find('div');
      jQuery(theDiv).hide('normal');
      jQuery(this).parent().parent().find('span.collapse').removeClass('collapse').addClass('expand');
        createCookie(theDiv.attr('id'), 0, 7);
    }
    jQuery('#' + id + ' .expand .sym').html(expandSym);
    expandCat(this, expandSym, collapseSym);
    return false;
  });
  jQuery('#' + id + ' .collapse').live('click', function() {
    collapseCat(this, expandSym, collapseSym);
    return false;
  });
}

function expandCat(symbol, expandSym, collapseSym) {
    var theDiv = jQuery(symbol).parent().find('div');
    jQuery(theDiv).html(collapsItems[jQuery(theDiv).attr('id')]).show('normal');
    jQuery(symbol).removeClass('expand').addClass('collapse');
    jQuery(symbol).find('.sym').html(collapseSym);
  createCookie(theDiv.attr('id'), 1, 7);
}
function collapseCat(symbol, expandSym, collapseSym) {
    var theDiv = jQuery(symbol).parent().find('div');
    jQuery(theDiv).hide('normal');
    jQuery(symbol).removeClass('collapse').addClass('expand');
    jQuery(symbol).find('.sym').html(expandSym);
  createCookie(theDiv.attr('id'), 0, 7);
}
addExpandCollapse('widget-collapscat-3-top','&#x25BA;', '&#x25BC;', 0)// ]]&gt;
          </script>
